 &lt;h2 class="hup_h2_title"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;100 MG Sour Diesel CBD TERPENES&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;
 &lt;div&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Rich Broad-Spectrum CBD Terps + Pure Cannabidiol + VG&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;This 100MG &lt;/span&gt;CBD Terpenes Oil&lt;span&gt; has been infused with &lt;/span&gt;CBD Sour Diesel Terpenes&lt;span&gt;. Terpenes are considered the main building blocks of any plant essential oils, and contribute to the scent, flavors, and effect. This blend of pure &lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href="https://www.greenroadsworld.com/collections/cbd-cannabis-oils"&gt;CBD oil&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span&gt; and &lt;/span&gt;broad spectrum CBD terpenes oil&lt;span&gt;contains a vegetable glycerin base and causes a powerful entourage effect, with a unique floral flavor. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;Our oil is made in America and compounded by a licensed pharmacist with 20 years + experience. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;The &lt;/span&gt;CBD Sour Diesel Terpenes: 100 MG&lt;span&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;are a low concentration of CBD. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;Each drop has approximately .3 MG of CBD&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;CBD Uses&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;Hemp has been used for thousands of years. At the time, the science behind hemp could not explain why it worked. However, people believed it to be a powerful &lt;/span&gt;plant.&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Now…&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;Modern day science explains the powers of hemp and why years ago it was used for so many different purposes. The hemp plant produces compounds called cannabinoids. These cannabinoids help create balance in your endocannabinoid system. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;What Happens If Your Endocannabinoid System Is Out Of Balance?&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;If your endocannabinoid system is out of balance, it can lead to symptoms such as inflammation, chronic pain, headaches and other, more serious conditions. These conditions come from &lt;/span&gt;Clinical Endocannabinoid Deficiency&lt;span&gt; (CECD). &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Product Facts:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;ul&gt;
 &lt;li&gt;Serving size: 2-3 Drops&lt;/li&gt;
 &lt;li&gt;Serving Per Bottle: 100&lt;/li&gt;
 &lt;li&gt;Concentration: Each drop has approximately .3 MG of CBD&lt;/li&gt;
 &lt;/ul&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Ingredients&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;CBD Oil, Hemp Seed Oil, 99% Pure CBD Crystalline Isolate, Kosher-Grade Vegetable Glycerin.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;How Much CBD Sour Diesel Terpenes: 100 MG CBD Oil Should I Take?&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;Each person may require a different concentration depending on internal factors.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Sublingual&lt;span&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;b&gt;Directions:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;ol&gt;
 &lt;li&gt;&lt;span&gt;Squeeze the dropper top to fill the pipette with oil.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
 &lt;li&gt;&lt;span&gt;Place 1-3 drops under the tongue.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
 &lt;li&gt;&lt;span&gt;Hold for 30 seconds before swallowing.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
 &lt;/ol&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;NOTE:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;Consult your physician before taking any new dietary supplements. Must be 18+ years older to consume.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

          <h3 itemprop="name">

          <div class="yotpo bottomLine" data-appkey="KDVqJMiCQPeWNeRKUiFXgKhIUwKs4lk1KxhoGNIn" data-bread-crumbs="CBD;" data-description='&lt;meta charset="utf-8"&gt;
 &lt;h2 class="hup_h2_title"&gt;CBD Froggies – Assorted Flavored CBD Edibles&lt;/h2&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;The CBD Froggies (100MG) are edibles made up of corn syrup, citric acid, gelatin, sugar, infused with pharmaceutical-grade cannabidiol.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;These &lt;/span&gt;CBD Froggies&lt;span&gt; have been infused with 100MG of CBD. Terpenes are considered the &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;main building blocks of any plant essential oils, and contribute to the scent, flavors, and colors. This blend of pure CBD oil and broad-spectrum terpenes is vegetable glycerin base and causes a powerful entourage effect, with a unique floral flavor.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;Our CBD Froggies are made in America and developed by a licensed pharmacist with 20 years + experience. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;The &lt;/span&gt;100MG CBD Froggies&lt;span&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;are a low dosage of CBD. If you are new to CBD, the &lt;/span&gt;100MG CBD Froggies&lt;span&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;would be the perfect choice for you.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;CBD Uses&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;CBD has been used for thousands of years by doctors to help their patients. At the time, the science behind hemp could not explain why it worked. However, | 100MG (4×25 MG) their patients believed it to be a powerful plant with healing abilities.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Now…&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

 &lt;h1&gt;&lt;b&gt;Kanger TOGO Mini All In One Starter Kit&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/h1&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;span&gt;The &lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;http://www.vapordna.com/Kanger-s/1920.htm&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;noopener noreferrer&quot;&gt;&lt;inline&gt;Kanger&lt;/inline&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span&gt; TOGO Mini is the &lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;http://www.vapordna.com/Whats-New-Devices-s/2489.htm&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;noopener noreferrer&quot;&gt;&lt;inline&gt;new &lt;/inline&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span&gt;All In One Starter Kit that addresses the shortcomings of ultra compact AIOs by packing in a tremendous tank capacity of 3.8 milliliters powered by a direct voltage based output. Based directly from the CUPTI and Argo platforms, Kanger's TOGO Mini maintains the side by side.design while integrating a premium textured finish. Ultra compact in size, the TOGO Mini squeezes in an ample 1600 mAh integrated battery that is charged at a maximal rate of 1A to ensure minimal downtime. Output of the TOGO Mini features a direct voltage output based on resistance and battery state, with a minimum atomizer resistance of 0.15 ohms. The system gives feedback off of a minimalist LED battery screen consisting of five vertically arranged LEDs that provide battery life. The tank system of the TOGO Mini sits directly adjacent to the chipset, with a maximum tank capacity of 3.8 milliliters, filled via a threaded top fill system. The coil structure utilized within is the tried and true CLOCC family that debuted with the CUPTI platform, and included in each set is a 0.5 ohm SS316L coil and a 1.0 ohm NiChrome MTL coil, catering to a well balanced and flavor orientated output, respectively.          else if (/KHTML|WebKit|iCab/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
             var DOMLoadTimer = setInterval(function () {

                     callback();
                     clearInterval(DOMLoadTimer);
                 }
             }, 10);
         }else{
             /* Other web browsers */
             window.onload = callback;
         }
     };

 &lt;div id=&quot;ProductDetail_ProductDetails_div&quot;&gt;
 &lt;h1&gt;&lt;b&gt;SMOK TFV12 Baby Prince Sub-Ohm Tank&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/h1&gt;
 &lt;span id=&quot;product_description&quot; itemprop=&quot;description&quot;&gt;&lt;br&gt;The&lt;span&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;http://www.vapordna.com/SMOKtech-s/1932.htm&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;noopener noreferrer&quot;&gt;&lt;inline&gt;SMOK&lt;/inline&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span&gt; &lt;/span&gt;TFV12 Baby Prince Sub-Ohm Tank enters the market as the most capable Sub-Ohm Tank ever released, asserting itself as the upgrading version of the TFV8 Baby Beast, presenting unprecedented vapor and flavor possibilities. Following up on the world's most popular Sub-Ohm Tank of 2016 with the TFV8 platform and its smaller editions, the TFV12 Baby Prince elevates the vape tank segment even greater, capable of utilizing the&lt;span&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://www.vapordna.com/SMOK-TFV8-Baby-Beast-Replacement-Coil-p/tfv8bc.htm&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;noopener noreferrer&quot;&gt;&lt;inline&gt;V8 Baby Coils&lt;/inline&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span&gt; &lt;/span&gt;that we all know and love. The chassis design of the TFV12 Baby Prince features multiple diameters, measuring 22mm at the base and 26mm at the widest point. The new press to open Top Fill System that isn't featured from the previous editions is fully implemented into the TFV12 Baby Prince, with a single fill port and a maximum tank capacity of 4.5 milliliters with the convex glass and 2 milliliters with the standard glass. The Baby Prince comes with three coils, the V8 Baby-Q4 0.4 ohm, rated at 30 to 65W and recommended at 50 to 60W, the new V8 Baby T12 Red Light Duodecuple Coil Head 0.15 ohm, rated at 50 to 80W and recommended at 60 to 80W, the V8 Baby Mesh Coil Head 0.15ohm, rated at 40 to 80W and recommended at 60 to 70W. The V8 Baby T12 Red Light Duodecuple Coil head lights up red when firing the device. Airflow for the TFV12 Baby Prince is configured around the base of the chassis, providing ample airflow even for the maximal range of the atomizer. Heralding in the newest generation of SMOK atomizers, the TFV12 Baby Prince Sub-Ohm Tank makes a bold but accurate assertion as the&lt;span&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;http://www.vapordna.com/Whats-New-Sub-Ohm-Tanks-s/2486.htm&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;noopener noreferrer&quot;&gt;&lt;inline&gt;premiere cloud chasing tank&lt;/inline&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span&gt; &lt;/span&gt;on the market.&lt;span&gt;&lt;inline&gt;&lt;inline&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/inline&gt;&lt;/inline&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;

         else if (/KHTML|WebKit|iCab/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
             var DOMLoadTimer = setInterval(function () {
                 if (/loaded|complete/i.test(document.readyState)) {
                     callback();
                     clearInterval(DOMLoadTimer);
                 }
             }, 10);
         }else{
             /* Other web browsers */
             window.onload = callback;
         }
     };

          <h3 itemprop="name">
           SMPL 2.0 (REMmod)
          </h3>
          <div class="yotpo bottomLine" data-appkey="KDVqJMiCQPeWNeRKUiFXgKhIUwKs4lk1KxhoGNIn" data-bread-crumbs="Mechanical Mods;" data-description="&lt;meta charset=&quot;utf-8&quot;&gt;&lt;meta charset=&quot;utf-8&quot;&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;The SMPL 2.0 Mod from REM Creations is one of the smallest &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;—&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt; and by far the simplest &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;—&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt; mechanical mods ever made. An update to the original SMPL mod, this new 2.0 version features a hybrid connection for direct battery / atomizer contact, a simple yet effective button assembly, and a stunning minimalist design. If you only ever own one mechanical mod, the SMPL 2.0 should be at the top of your list.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;meta charset=&quot;utf-8&quot;&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;This 18650 mod only works with 18650 batteries, eliminating potential voltage drop from extention tubes and additional seams and threads. Only the button assembly screws on and off, and also works to adjust for battery rattle. The recessed button ensures that this mod won't fire in your pocket or bag, and is made from rhodium plated stainless steel for optimal performance.&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;Due to the hybrid style atomizer connection, the length of your atomizer's threads will determine whether you can use it with the SMPL 2.0. Please be sure to NEVER use flat post atomizers (such as the Aspire Atlantis) with any hybrid style mods.&lt;/p&gt;" data-domain="the-steam-co.myshopify.com" data-image-url="//cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/0290/8697/products/smpl2.0_large.jpg%3Fv=1456167990" data-name="SMPL 2.0 (REMmod)" data-product-id="533776961" data-product-models="533776961" data-url="">
